# Benchmark: [WAL DISK] Recovery Replay - Sequential Read

**Date:** 2026-01-03 13:07:50
**Scenario:** Sequential Read - Simulates Replica Catch-up or Crash Recovery

---

| Property | Value |
|----------|-------|
| **Name** | **WAL** |
| **Mount Point** | `/wal` |
| **Device** | `/dev/md1` |
| **Volumes** | `nvme1n1, nvme4n1, nvme6n1, nvme7n1, nvme10n1, nvme13n1, nvme14n1, nvme16n1` |

## Command 1: fio

### Command
```bash
fio --name=wal_read_replay --filename=/wal/bench_wal_replay --size=5G --time_based --runtime=60s --ioengine=libaio --direct=1 --bs=1M --rw=read --iodepth=8 --numjobs=1 --group_reporting
```
